# ============================================================
# STREAMING OS META OVERVIEW
# ============================================================

status: canonical-draft
system: streaming-os
layer: meta
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

# ============================================================
# 1. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

This document gives the meta overview
for StreamingOS.

The meta layer records:
- progress summaries
- verification notes
- review notes
- handoff notes
- closeout markers
- restart markers
- navigation guides
- recent delta reflection notes

for the current StreamingOS design state.

# ============================================================
# 2. META POSITION
# ============================================================

StreamingOS meta must support:
- design progress visibility
- precision progress visibility
- freeze-phase visibility
- review visibility
- handoff visibility
- closeout and stop visibility
- restart navigation visibility
- recent platform/device support reflection visibility
- recent international support reflection visibility
- recent delta-bundle visibility

# ============================================================
# 3. CROSS-DEVICE META SUPPORT
# ============================================================

StreamingOS meta shall preserve
the interpretation that StreamingOS
is a cross-device platform.

Supported device classes:
- iPhone
- Android
- PC
- tablet

Meta implication:
- summaries,
  handoff notes,
  closeout notes,
  restart notes,
  and delta notes
  must not silently fall back
  to one-device-only interpretation
- creator,
  viewer,
  moderation,
  notification,
  and corporate oversight meanings
  must remain cross-device
  in meta summaries as well

# ============================================================
# 4. INTERNATIONAL META SUPPORT
# ============================================================

StreamingOS meta shall preserve
the interpretation that StreamingOS supports:
- multilingual operation
- multi-currency handling
- nation-aware currency display inside Civilization

Meta implication:
- summary documents must keep
  multilingual interpretation visible
- summary documents must keep
  multi-currency interpretation visible
- summary documents must keep
  canonical monetary meaning vs display currency meaning
  distinguishable

# ============================================================
# 5. META DISTINCTIONS
# ============================================================

StreamingOS meta must preserve:
- design completion vs implementation completion
- precision progress vs freeze progress
- handoff state vs restart guidance
- delta reflection vs implementation kickoff
- canonical monetary meaning vs display currency meaning
- multilingual platform interpretation vs optional wording
- cross-device platform interpretation vs single-device assumption

# ============================================================
# 6. CANONICAL FIXED STATEMENT
# ============================================================

StreamingOS meta is fixed
as a multilingual,
multi-currency,
cross-device meta layer
for creator,
viewer,
moderation,
notification,
corporate oversight,
and monetization design interpretation
across iPhone,
Android,
PC,
and tablet environments.




<!-- ========================================================= -->
<!-- SOURCE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/06.streaming-os/900.meta/000_STREAMING_META_INDEX.md -->

<!-- SOURCE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/06.streaming-os/900.meta/010.current-status-and-handoff/9001000_STREAMING_OS_CURRENT_STATUS_AND_HANDOFF.md -->

# ============================================================
# STREAMING OS CURRENT STATUS AND HANDOFF
# ============================================================

status: canonical-handoff
system: streaming-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

# ============================================================
# 1. CURRENT POSITION
# ============================================================

StreamingOS has been structurally deepened across:
- 019.interface
- 020.architecture
- 030.model
- 040.runtime
- 050.flow
- 060.integration
- 070.operations
- 080.policy
- 090.security
- 100.infrastructure
- 120.implementation

This means the current state is no longer
a thin conceptual draft.
It is now a multi-layer semantic design base.

# ============================================================
# 2. WHAT HAS BEEN FIXED
# ============================================================

The following major meanings have been fixed:

- only formal Civilization subjects with Civilization IDs
  may become stream principals
- company official streams use company ownership by default
- performers remain distinct from ownership
- archive and clip assets remain canonically owned by StreamingOS
- YouTube is treated as an external publication destination
- internal native reactions exist
- rankings exist for videos,
  streams,
  and broadcasters
- internal ad data and insertion are controlled by StreamingOS
- Ai(human) emotional auto tipping exists
- Ai(robot) does not emotionally auto tip by default
- Ai-origin tipping uses Civilization national currency
- beneficiary-side national currency conversion exists
- BusinessOS linkage may exist
- ERP is not the current downstream target
- governance restrictions preserve history rather than erase it

# ============================================================
# 3. WHAT IS ALREADY STRUCTURED
# ============================================================

Already structured at semantic design level:
- ownership layer
- performer layer
- session lifecycle layer
- archive / clip layer
- external publication layer
- monetization layer
- auto tipping layer
- reaction / ranking layer
- ad layer
- governance layer
- operational layer
- security layer
- infrastructure layer
- implementation responsibility layer

# ============================================================
# 4. WHAT IS NOT YET FINALIZED
# ============================================================

The following are still not final:
- exact physical DB schema
- exact API request / response contracts
- exact runtime workers and schedulers
- exact infra topology
- exact class/module/package structure
- exact UI wireframes
- exact review workflow screens
- exact business linkage payloads

# ============================================================
# 5. RECOMMENDED NEXT STEPS
# ============================================================

Most natural next steps:

1.
Deepen 030.model further into more exact record families

2.
Create exact API contracts
for:
- principal selection
- session control
- archive / clip management
- YouTube publish
- tipping
- auto tipping
- reactions
- rankings
- ad management

3.
Create implementation-facing module boundaries

4.
Create UI wireframe-grade screen specifications

5.
Create review / validation / consistency pass
across the current StreamingOS tree

# ============================================================
# 6. ROOT READING ORDER
# ============================================================

Recommended reading order:
- 000_STREAMING_OS_OVERVIEW.md
- 00_STREAMING_OS_INTEGRATED_REBUILT.md
- 020.architecture/000_STREAMING_ARCHITECTURE_OVERVIEW.md
- 019.interface/000_STREAMING_INTERFACE_OVERVIEW.md
- 030.model/000_STREAMING_MODEL_OVERVIEW.md
- 040.runtime/000_STREAMING_RUNTIME_OVERVIEW.md
- 050.flow/000_STREAMING_FLOW_OVERVIEW.md
- 060.integration/000_STREAMING_INTEGRATION_OVERVIEW.md
- 070.operations/000_STREAMING_OPERATIONS_OVERVIEW.md
- 080.policy/000_STREAMING_POLICY_OVERVIEW.md
- 090.security/000_STREAMING_SECURITY_OVERVIEW.md
- 100.infrastructure/000_STREAMING_INFRASTRUCTURE_OVERVIEW.md
- 120.implementation/000_STREAMING_IMPLEMENTATION_OVERVIEW.md

# ============================================================
# 7. HANDOFF STATEMENT
# ============================================================

StreamingOS is currently in a strong semantic-architecture state.
The next work should focus on
precision,
exact contracts,
and consistency,
rather than reopening core concepts unnecessarily.

# ============================================================
# STREAMING OS INDEPENDENCE COMPLETION SUMMARY
# ============================================================

status: canonical-meta
system: streaming-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

# ============================================================
# 1. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

This document summarizes
the major previously under-separated StreamingOS areas
that have now been explicitly separated
into independent design domains.

# ============================================================
# 2. COMPLETED INDEPENDENCE AREAS
# ============================================================

The following major areas,
which were previously implicit,
thin,
or not independently structured enough,
have now been separated explicitly.

creator-side areas:
- creator my page
- video upload and studio
- channel management
- creator analytics
- corporate channel and affiliated streamer handling

viewer-side areas:
- discovery and home
- search and history
- subscription and follow
- live watch and waiting room
- playlist and watch queue

moderation / governance-side areas:
- review and moderation pipeline
- review and rights queue
- comment moderation
- report and appeal
- ban and restoration
- review notification and escalation

platform-support areas:
- notification and inbox
- recommendation and search integration
- creator analytics integration
- corporate oversight integration
- creator / viewer / moderation / notification / corporate
  operations,
  policy,
  security,
  infrastructure,
  and implementation responsibilities

# ============================================================
# 3. LAYER-WIDE SEPARATION STATUS
# ============================================================

The following layers now explicitly include
the newly separated responsibility groups:

- 019.interface
- 020.architecture
- 030.model
- 050.flow
- 060.integration
- 070.operations
- 080.policy
- 090.security
- 100.infrastructure
- 120.implementation

# ============================================================
# 4. WHAT THIS MEANS
# ============================================================

StreamingOS is no longer only:
- stream/session design
- YouTube push design
- tipping/reaction/ranking design

It is now also explicitly designed as:
- a creator platform
- a viewer platform
- a moderation and restoration platform
- a notification and review-alert platform
- a company/affiliation oversight platform

# ============================================================
# 5. WHAT REMAINS AFTER THIS
# ============================================================

After this independence pass,
the major remaining precision work is not
"what domains exist?"
but rather:
- exact DDL expansion for the newly separated domains
- exact API contract expansion for the newly separated domains
- exact runtime worker / job mapping
- exact UI wireframe-grade screen design
- exact migration order and implementation packaging

# ============================================================
# 6. CANONICAL META STATEMENT
# ============================================================

The major previously under-separated StreamingOS platform areas
have now been independently structured.

Subsequent work should focus on
precision,
exact contracts,
exact DDL,
and implementation-facing refinement,
rather than re-opening the existence of these major domains.

# ============================================================
# STREAMING OS PRECISION PROGRESS SUMMARY
# ============================================================

status: canonical-meta
system: streaming-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

# ============================================================
# 1. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

This document summarizes
the precision-phase progress of StreamingOS
after major domain independence was established.

# ============================================================
# 2. PRECISION PHASE STATUS
# ============================================================

The current precision phase has advanced across:
- exact API contract expansion
- exact DDL candidate expansion
- runtime / worker / job exact mapping
- root reflection across major layers
- multilingual support reflection
- multi-currency support reflection
- cross-device support reflection

# ============================================================
# 3. API EXACT CONTRACT STATUS
# ============================================================

Exact API contract coverage now includes:

base platform:
- principal and session
- archive and publish
- tipping and auto tipping
- reaction, ranking, and internal ads

newly expanded platform areas:
- creator platform
- viewer discovery and continuity
- moderation and appeal
- notification and platform events
- corporate channel and affiliation

position:
API intent is fixed at request / response payload level,
while still transport-neutral.

# ============================================================
# 4. EXACT DDL STATUS
# ============================================================

Exact DDL candidate coverage now includes:

base domains:
- principals and sessions
- assets and external publish
- tipping, currency conversion, and auto tipping
- reactions, rankings, and internal ads

newly expanded domains:
- creator platform
- viewer discovery and continuity
- comment / report / appeal
- notification / platform event
- channel / corporate oversight

position:
Table-level exact DDL candidate coverage
has been expanded meaningfully,
but executable migration freeze is not yet final.

# ============================================================
# 5. RUNTIME EXACT MAPPING STATUS
# ============================================================

Runtime / worker / job mapping now includes:

base runtime areas:
- session runtime
- archive and clip runtime
- external publish runtime
- monetization and auto tipping runtime

newly expanded runtime areas:
- creator platform runtime jobs
- viewer discovery and continuity runtime jobs
- moderation and appeal runtime jobs
- notification and event runtime jobs
- corporate channel and affiliation runtime jobs

position:
Semantic worker/job mapping is now largely fixed,
though scheduler syntax and deployment binding are still later work.

# ============================================================
# 6. PLATFORM / INTERNATIONAL SUPPORT STATUS
# ============================================================

Platform and international support is now reflected as:
- multilingual support
- multi-currency handling
- nation-aware currency display
- iPhone support
- Android support
- PC support
- tablet support

position:
These are now reflected
not only at constitution/root level,
but also across major architectural layers.

# ============================================================
# 7. WHAT IS NOW CONSIDERED SUBSTANTIALLY FIXED
# ============================================================

The following are now substantially fixed at design level:
- major domain independence
- layer-wide responsibility separation
- exact API payload intent
- major table-family DDL candidate direction
- runtime job/worker category separation
- multilingual platform interpretation
- multi-currency platform interpretation
- cross-device platform interpretation

# ============================================================
# 8. WHAT STILL REMAINS
# ============================================================

Major remaining precision work includes:
- final executable DDL freeze
- migration order freeze
- exact auth / access-control mapping
- exact scheduler / queue binding
- wireframe-grade UI precision
- implementation package / module naming freeze

# ============================================================
# 9. CANONICAL META STATEMENT
# ============================================================

StreamingOS has now progressed
from major domain separation
into meaningful precision-phase design.

Subsequent work should focus on
freeze-grade precision,
not on rediscovering major domain boundaries.

# 1. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

This document lists the most natural
next precision targets for StreamingOS
after the current API / DDL / runtime expansion.

# ============================================================
# 2. HIGHEST PRIORITY TARGETS
# ============================================================

Highest priority next targets:

- executable DDL freeze candidate set
- migration order design
- auth / access-control exact mapping
- queue / scheduler exact mapping
- wireframe-grade UI precision
- implementation module/package freeze

# ============================================================
# 3. DDL TARGETS
# ============================================================

DDL next targets:
- constraint refinement
- unique-key tightening
- audit column standardization
- soft-delete / hidden-state exact rule
- trigger strategy freeze
- migration dependency ordering

# ============================================================

# ============================================================

API next targets:
- actor authorization rules per endpoint
- error payload conventions
- pagination conventions
- filter/sort exact fields
- write-operation idempotency rules

# ============================================================

# ============================================================

Runtime next targets:
- queue names
- retry policy
- backoff policy
- worker ownership mapping
- job priority mapping
- scheduled refresh windows

# ============================================================
# STREAMING OS ROOT PRECISION REFLECTION SUMMARY
# ============================================================

status: canonical-meta
system: streaming-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

# ============================================================
# 1. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

This document summarizes
the root-level precision progress
of StreamingOS after major independence
and precision-phase expansion.

# ============================================================
# 2. COMPLETED LARGE STEPS
# ============================================================

The following large steps are now substantially completed:

step_01:
major domain independence established across:
- interface
- architecture
- model
- flow
- integration
- operations
- policy
- security
- infrastructure
- implementation

step_02:
new creator / viewer / moderation / notification / corporate areas
added as independently structured domains

step_03:
precision-phase expansion added across:
- exact API contracts
- exact DDL candidates
- runtime / worker / job mapping
- scheduler / queue / retry mapping
- access-control exact mapping
- migration order / dependency freeze
- screen inventory / transition map
- wireframe block definitions
- module / package split freeze

# ============================================================
# 3. WHAT ROOT-LEVEL READING NOW MEANS
# ============================================================

Reading StreamingOS from the root now means
the system is no longer only:
- stream/session design
- YouTube push design
- tipping/reaction/ranking design

It is now also explicitly:
- creator platform design
- viewer platform design
- moderation / restoration platform design
- notification / alert platform design
- company / affiliation oversight platform design
- implementation-facing precision design

# ============================================================
# 4. ROOT-LEVEL PRECISION STATUS
# ============================================================

root_precision_status:
- semantic_domain_independence
  substantially fixed
- exact_api_payload_intent
  substantially fixed
- exact_table_family_direction
  substantially fixed
- runtime_job_family_direction
  substantially fixed
- scheduler_queue_retry_direction
  substantially fixed
- access_control_direction
  substantially fixed
- screen inventory direction
  substantially fixed
- wireframe block direction
  substantially fixed
- package/module split direction
  substantially fixed

# ============================================================
# 5. WHAT STILL REMAINS AFTER THIS
# ============================================================

The most natural remaining work is now:
- final executable DDL freeze
- final migration script sequencing
- final queue / scheduler binding detail
- final auth / RLS / actor-binding detail
- wireframe-to-screen-spec precision
- module-to-source-tree precision
- implementation kickoff packaging

# ============================================================
# 6. CANONICAL META STATEMENT
# ============================================================

StreamingOS has progressed beyond
domain discovery and mid-level structure.

It is now in a late precision-design state,
where the remaining work is mostly
freeze-grade implementation refinement.

# ============================================================
# STREAMING OS CURRENT POSITION AND NEXT PHASE
# ============================================================

status: canonical-meta
system: streaming-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

# ============================================================
# 1. CURRENT POSITION
# ============================================================

Current position:
StreamingOS is now after
major independence design
and after major precision expansion.

This means the current design stage is best understood as:

late_precision_design

not:
- early conceptual design
- missing-domain discovery
- loosely grouped platform structure

# ============================================================
# 2. BEST NEXT PHASE
# ============================================================

Best next phase:

freeze_phase

recommended order:
- final executable DDL freeze
- final API freeze
- final auth / access-control / RLS freeze
- final runtime queue / scheduler freeze
- final screen spec freeze
- implementation kickoff structure freeze

# ============================================================
# 3. WHAT SHOULD NOT BE RE-OPENED LIGHTLY
# ============================================================

The following should not be reopened lightly:
- major platform area existence
- creator/viewer/moderation/notification/corporate separation
- core platform responsibility split
- major runtime job category split
- major package/module split

# ============================================================
# 4. WHAT IS STILL OPEN FOR REFINEMENT
# ============================================================

The following remain open for refinement:
- exact constraint wording
- exact endpoint field naming
- exact pagination/filter allowlists
- exact retry counts and intervals
- exact screen block order
- exact package names / source tree conventions

# ============================================================
# STREAMING OS FREEZE PHASE SUMMARY
# ============================================================

status: canonical-meta
system: streaming-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

# ============================================================
# 1. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

This document summarizes
the freeze-phase progress of StreamingOS
after major domain independence
and precision-phase expansion.

# ============================================================
# 2. FREEZE-PHASE POSITION
# ============================================================

StreamingOS has now moved into
freeze-oriented design work.

This means the current design state includes:
- executable DDL freeze direction
- final API freeze direction
- final RLS / auth freeze direction
- final scheduler binding freeze direction
- multilingual platform interpretation freeze
- multi-currency platform interpretation freeze
- cross-device platform interpretation freeze

The design is no longer in a domain-discovery stage.

# ============================================================
# 3. WHAT IS NOW FREEZE-GRADE OR NEAR FREEZE-GRADE
# ============================================================

The following areas are now freeze-grade
or near freeze-grade at semantic design level:

api:
- endpoint catalog
- endpoint naming style
- success response envelope
- error semantics
- pagination / filter / sort conventions
- idempotency semantics
- actor / authorization error distinction

data:
- exact DDL candidate expansion
- executable DDL freeze direction
- migration order and dependency freeze

security:
- actor / role matrix
- access-control exact mapping
- table-family RLS binding direction

runtime:
- worker / job category separation
- scheduler / queue / retry exact mapping
- scheduler binding freeze direction

ui:
- screen inventory
- transition map
- wireframe block definitions

implementation:
- module and package split freeze

platform_and_international:
- multilingual interpretation
- multi-currency interpretation
- nation-aware display currency interpretation
- iPhone support interpretation
- Android support interpretation
- PC support interpretation
- tablet support interpretation

# ============================================================
# 4. WHAT THIS MEANS PRACTICALLY
# ============================================================

StreamingOS is now positioned so that
implementation kickoff can be planned
without reopening major semantic boundaries.

In practical terms:
- major platform areas are fixed
- major API families are fixed
- major table families are fixed
- major runtime families are fixed
- major access-control intent is fixed
- major UI surface inventory is fixed
- multilingual support is fixed as a platform capability
- multi-currency support is fixed as a platform capability
- cross-device support is fixed across iPhone,
  Android,
  PC,
  and tablet

# ============================================================
# 5. WHAT STILL REMAINS AFTER FREEZE-PHASE SUMMARY
# ============================================================

The main remaining work after this summary is:
- executable SQL block polishing for direct execution
- transport-specific API binding
- RLS policy SQL drafting
- scheduler / queue vendor binding
- screen-spec ordering refinement
- implementation kickoff package/tree concretization
- final verification pass across root layer files

# ============================================================
# 6. CANONICAL META STATEMENT
# ============================================================

StreamingOS has progressed beyond
major domain separation
and beyond broad precision expansion.

It is now in a freeze-oriented design state,
where remaining work is primarily
execution-grade refinement and verification.

recommended_order:

- step_05_runtime_binding_decision

  or mixed

- is cross-layer aligned

<!-- SOURCE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/06.streaming-os/900.meta/025.final-design-review/9002710_STREAMING_OS_SEMANTIC_CONSISTENCY_REVIEW.md -->

# ============================================================
# STREAMING OS SEMANTIC CONSISTENCY REVIEW
# ============================================================

status: canonical-meta
system: streaming-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

# ============================================================
# 1. REVIEW TARGET
# ============================================================

semantic_targets:
- principal vs performer
- ownership vs participation
- archive existence vs external publication
- formal tipping vs emotional auto tipping
- reaction activity vs ranking result
- moderation restriction vs restoration
- creator self-state vs public channel state
- viewer continuity vs recommendation output
- company ownership vs affiliated participation
- canonical monetary meaning vs display currency meaning
- shared multilingual capability vs ad hoc wording
- cross-device platform meaning vs single-device interpretation

# ============================================================
# 2. REVIEW QUESTIONS
# ============================================================

review_questions:
- Is each semantic distinction still explicit?
- Has any later document silently collapsed an earlier distinction?
- Do creator/viewer/moderation/notification/corporate meanings remain separate?
- Do summary/meta docs preserve the same interpretation as detailed docs?
- Is multilingual support treated as platform capability rather than optional wording?
- Is multi-currency support treated as canonical interpretation rather than display-only decoration?
- Is cross-device support treated as iPhone / Android / PC / tablet platform scope rather than smartphone-only scope?

# ============================================================
# 3. PASS CONDITIONS
# ============================================================

pass_conditions:
- no major semantic contradiction across layers
- no silent merge of distinct meanings
- no old stream-only interpretation remaining in root summaries
- no freeze doc redefining ownership or review semantics
- no document collapses canonical monetary meaning into display currency meaning
- no document treats multilingual support as an optional afterthought
- no document reintroduces one-device-only interpretation

# ============================================================

result:
- root scope is no longer stream-only
- creator platform meaning is reflected

# ============================================================
# STREAMING OS HANDOFF CURRENT SCOPE
# ============================================================

status: canonical-handoff
system: streaming-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

# ============================================================
# 1. CANONICAL CURRENT SCOPE
# ============================================================

StreamingOS currently covers all of the following
as explicit internal platform scope:

creator-side:
- creator my page
- channel management
- upload and studio
- creator analytics
- creator settings

viewer-side:
- home / discovery
- search
- waiting room
- live watch
- archive watch
- clip watch
- follow / history / playlist / queue

moderation-side:
- AI review
- human review
- rights/safety/age/ad review dimensions
- report handling
- comment moderation
- appeal
- restoration

notification-side:
- creator notifications
- viewer notifications
- review alerts
- escalation alerts

corporate-side:
- official company channel
- affiliated streamer visibility
- corporate oversight
- company-side issue visibility
- company-side monetization visibility

platform_and_international_scope:
- multilingual operation
- multi-currency handling
- nation-aware currency display
- iPhone support
- Android support
- PC support
- tablet support

# ============================================================
# 2. EXPLICIT NON-SCOPE FOR NOW
# ============================================================

Not yet in implementation scope:
- standalone video editing application implementation
- real queue vendor selection
- real transport/API framework binding
- actual DB deployment/migration execution




<!-- ========================================================= -->

# ============================================================
# STREAMING OS HANDOFF RESTART GUIDE
# ============================================================

status: canonical-handoff
system: streaming-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

# ============================================================
# 1. IF RESTARTING IN A NEW CHAT
# ============================================================

Recommended restart order:

1.
Read root files:
- 000_STREAMING_OS_OVERVIEW.md
- 000_STREAMING_OS_INDEX.md
- 00_STREAMING_OS_INTEGRATED_REBUILT.md

2.
Read precision/freeze summaries:
- 9002300_STREAMING_OS_PRECISION_PROGRESS_SUMMARY.md
- 9002500_STREAMING_OS_FREEZE_PHASE_SUMMARY.md
- 9002800_STREAMING_OS_ROOT_REVIEW_RESULT_SUMMARY.md

3.
Read platform/international interpretation entry points:
- 0100004_STREAMING_OS_PLATFORM_AND_INTERNATIONAL_SUPPORT_ADDITIVE_NOTE.md
- 000_STREAMING_OS_CONSTITUTION_OVERVIEW.md
- 000_STREAMING_ARCHITECTURE_OVERVIEW.md
- 000_STREAMING_INTERFACE_OVERVIEW.md
- 000_STREAMING_MODEL_OVERVIEW.md
- 000_STREAMING_RUNTIME_OVERVIEW.md

4.
Then choose one path:
- design refinement path
- implementation kickoff preparation path

# ============================================================
# 2. DESIGN REFINEMENT PATH
# ============================================================

If continuing design only:
- check final verification pass
- polish naming / numbering if needed
- polish field-level contract names if needed
- polish screen block ordering if needed
- keep multilingual / multi-currency / cross-device wording aligned

# ============================================================
# 3. IMPLEMENTATION KICKOFF PREPARATION PATH
# ============================================================

If preparing eventual implementation:
- start from executable DDL freeze docs
- then final API freeze docs
- then final RLS/auth freeze docs
- then final scheduler binding freeze docs
- then module/package split freeze docs

# ============================================================
# 4. IMPORTANT REMINDER
# ============================================================

Implementation has not started yet.

Do not assume:
- SQL has already been executed
- migrations already exist
- runtime queues already exist
- endpoint transport bindings already exist

Also do not assume
multilingual / multi-currency / cross-device support
is optional;
it is now part of the canonical interpretation.

# ============================================================
# 1. IMPORTANT NON-MISREAD RULES
# ============================================================

Do not misread the current state as:
- implementation complete
- SQL executed
- policy SQL completed
- scheduler infra selected
- UI fully designed at pixel level

Do read the current state as:
- design broad-complete
- precision broad-complete
- freeze-oriented documentation broad-complete
- implementation still intentionally deferred

# ============================================================

Do not collapse:
- creator platform into public channel only
- viewer platform into search only
- moderation into silent block only
- notification into generic inbox only
- corporate oversight into mere affiliation visibility

# ============================================================
# STREAMING OS MASTER CLOSEOUT REPORT
# ============================================================

status: canonical-master-closeout
system: streaming-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

# ============================================================
# 1. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

This document is the master closeout report
for the current StreamingOS design work.

It exists to provide one final,
top-level confirmation that the current design phase
has reached a safe,
reviewable,
handoffable stopping point.

# ============================================================
# 2. MASTER RESULT
# ============================================================

master_result:
PASS_AT_DESIGN_LEVEL

# ============================================================
# 3. WHAT HAS BEEN ACHIEVED
# ============================================================

achieved:
- major platform domain separation completed
- creator-side platform scope explicitly structured
- viewer-side platform scope explicitly structured
- moderation / restoration scope explicitly structured
- notification / alert scope explicitly structured
- corporate / affiliation oversight scope explicitly structured
- precision-phase design broadly completed
- freeze-oriented design broadly completed
- final review / handoff / closeout / stop markers present
- multilingual platform interpretation reflected
- multi-currency platform interpretation reflected
- nation-aware currency display interpretation reflected
- cross-device support reflected across:
  - iPhone
  - Android
  - PC
  - tablet

# ============================================================
# 4. WHAT THIS RESULT DOES NOT MEAN
# ============================================================

this_result_does_not_mean:
- implementation started
- SQL executed
- migrations executed
- policy SQL completed
- API transport bound
- scheduler vendor selected
- UI implemented

# ============================================================
# 5. MASTER CLOSEOUT STATEMENT
# ============================================================

StreamingOS is design-broad-complete,
late-precision,
freeze-oriented,
multilingual,
multi-currency,
nation-aware in display currency,
cross-device across iPhone,
Android,
PC,
and tablet,
reviewed,
handoff-ready,
and safe to pause.

# ============================================================
# STREAMING OS MASTER DO AND DO NOT NOTE
# ============================================================

status: canonical-master-closeout
system: streaming-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

# ============================================================
# 1. DO
# ============================================================

do:
- read handoff summaries first
- read freeze summaries next
- use closeout and stop markers as current-position truth
- treat remaining work as refinement or later implementation-preparation only
- preserve multilingual interpretation
- preserve multi-currency interpretation
- preserve cross-device interpretation across iPhone,
  Android,
  PC,
  and tablet

# ============================================================
# 2. DO NOT
# ============================================================

do_not:
- assume implementation exists
- reopen major platform boundaries lightly
- collapse creator/viewer/moderation/notification/corporate meanings
- misread freeze docs as execution-complete
- misread executable-ddl-freeze as already-applied SQL
- treat multilingual / multi-currency / cross-device support as optional wording only

# ============================================================
# 3. MASTER RULE
# ============================================================

master_rule:
Interpret the current state as design-complete enough to stop,
not implementation-complete enough to run.

# ============================================================
# STREAMING OS PLATFORM AND INTERNATIONAL REFLECTION SUMMARY
# ============================================================

status: canonical-meta
system: streaming-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

# ============================================================
# 1. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

This document summarizes
the reflection of platform/device support
and international support
across StreamingOS.

# ============================================================
# 2. REFLECTED SUPPORT
# ============================================================

reflected_support:
- multilingual operation
- multi-currency handling
- nation-aware currency display
- iPhone support
- Android support
- PC support
- tablet support

# ============================================================
# 3. REFLECTION TARGETS
# ============================================================

reflection_targets:
- constitution
- root overview / index / integrated
- interface overview / index / integrated
- architecture overview / index / integrated
- model overview / index / integrated
- runtime overview / index / integrated
- flow overview / index / integrated
- integration overview / index / integrated
- operations overview / index / integrated
- policy overview / index / integrated
- security overview / index / integrated
- infrastructure overview / index / integrated
- implementation overview / index / integrated
- meta overview / index / integrated
- meta summaries / handoff / closeout / navigation / verification / review

# ============================================================
# 4. INTERPRETATION
# ============================================================

interpretation:
StreamingOS is no longer to be read
as a single-device,
single-language,
or single-currency platform.

It is now explicitly interpreted as:
- multilingual
- multi-currency
- nation-aware in display currency
- cross-device across:
  - iPhone
  - Android
  - PC
  - tablet

# ============================================================
# 5. DESIGN IMPLICATION
# ============================================================

design_implication:
These meanings apply across:
- creator platform interpretation
- viewer platform interpretation
- moderation interpretation
- notification interpretation
- corporate oversight interpretation
- monetization interpretation

They are not limited
to viewer pages only
or to later implementation decisions.

# ============================================================
# 6. CANONICAL META STATEMENT
# ============================================================

The current StreamingOS design set
has been updated so that
platform/device support
and international support
are explicitly reflected
across root,
major layers,
and meta summaries.

that the current reflection pass
for platform/device support
and international support
has been completed across the major StreamingOS design set.

- multilingual operation

- PC support
- tablet support

- constitution

- interface overview / index / integrated
- architecture overview / index / integrated
- model overview / index / integrated
- runtime overview / index / integrated
- flow overview / index / integrated
- integration overview / index / integrated

- implementation overview / index / integrated
- meta overview / index / integrated

# ============================================================

result_interpretation:

- multilingual
- multi-currency
- nation-aware in display currency
- cross-device across:
  - iPhone
  - Android
  - PC
  - tablet

- creator platform meaning
- viewer platform meaning
- moderation meaning
- notification meaning
- corporate oversight meaning
- monetization meaning

- settlement implementation is complete

- tablet client exists

not that implementation has started.

for multilingual support,

across iPhone,
Android,
PC,
and tablet
is considered complete
at the design-document interpretation level.

prepared_by: Zero

# ============================================================
# 1. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

This note records that the current root-entry interpretation
of StreamingOS has been updated.

# ============================================================

# ============================================================

StreamingOS root entry should now be read as:

- creator platform
- viewer platform
- moderation platform
- notification platform
- corporate oversight platform
- monetization platform
- multilingual platform
- multi-currency platform
- nation-aware currency display platform
- cross-device platform

# ============================================================

# ============================================================

- iPhone
- Android
- PC
- tablet

# ============================================================
# 4. SUPPORTED INTERNATIONAL CAPABILITIES
# ============================================================

- multilingual operation
- multi-currency handling
- nation-aware currency display

# ============================================================

# ============================================================

This is a design-interpretation completion note only.

It does not mean:
- implementation started
- clients already exist
- localization is implemented
- settlement logic is implemented

# ============================================================

At root-entry level,
StreamingOS is now explicitly fixed
as multilingual,
multi-currency,
nation-aware in display currency,
and cross-device across iPhone,
Android,
PC,
and tablet.

# ============================================================
# STREAMING OS PLATFORM AND INTERNATIONAL MASTER BUNDLE NOTE
# ============================================================

status: canonical-meta
system: streaming-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

# ============================================================
# 1. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

This note defines the master bundle
for the recent platform/device support
and international support reflection work
inside StreamingOS.

It exists so that the recent delta set
can be understood as one completed bundle,
not only as many separate notes.

# ============================================================
# 2. MASTER BUNDLE NAME
# ============================================================

master_bundle_name:
platform_and_international_reflection_bundle

# ============================================================
# 3. MASTER BUNDLE CONTENT
# ============================================================

master_bundle_content:
- multilingual operation reflection
- multi-currency handling reflection
- nation-aware currency display reflection
- iPhone support reflection
- Android support reflection
- PC support reflection
- tablet support reflection

# ============================================================
# 4. MASTER BUNDLE COVERAGE
# ============================================================

master_bundle_coverage:
- constitution
- root
- interface
- architecture
- model
- runtime
- flow
- integration
- operations
- policy
- security
- infrastructure
- implementation
- meta overview / index / integrated
- review summaries
- handoff summaries
- closeout summaries
- navigation summaries
- delta summaries
- delta closeout
- delta final stop

# ============================================================
# 5. MASTER BUNDLE INTERPRETATION
# ============================================================

master_bundle_interpretation:
StreamingOS must now be read consistently as:
- multilingual
- multi-currency
- nation-aware in display currency
- cross-device across:
  - iPhone
  - Android
  - PC
  - tablet

This interpretation applies across:
- creator platform meaning
- viewer platform meaning
- moderation meaning

- 053.platform-and-international-restart-flow-closeout
- 054.platform-and-international-theme-complete

# ============================================================
# 3. REOPEN RULE
# ============================================================

reopen_rule:
A later chat should not reopen
the controlled range
for concept rediscovery.

A later chat may only:
- read
- verify consistency
- extract handoff meaning
- prepare implementation-oriented followup
- refine wording without changing meaning

A later chat should not:
- re-scope the theme
- remove multilingual interpretation
- remove multi-currency interpretation
- remove nation-aware currency display interpretation
- remove iPhone / Android / PC / tablet interpretation
- collapse the restart flow
- replace the fixed entry order casually

# ============================================================
# 4. SAFE RESTART ORDER
# ============================================================

safe_restart_order:
- 9005300_STREAMING_OS_PLATFORM_AND_INTERNATIONAL_THEME_COMPLETE_NOTE.md
- 9005200_STREAMING_OS_PLATFORM_AND_INTERNATIONAL_RESTART_FLOW_CLOSEOUT_NOTE.md

- 9005000_STREAMING_OS_PLATFORM_AND_INTERNATIONAL_NEXT_CHAT_HANDOFF.md

# ============================================================
# 5. IMPORTANT LIMIT
# ============================================================

important_limit:
This note does not block
later implementation preparation.

It only blocks
unnecessary conceptual reopening
of the already completed design bundle.

# ============================================================
# 6. CANONICAL NOTE
# ============================================================

The recent platform/device support
and international support theme
for StreamingOS
should now be treated
as closed against casual redesign.

# ============================================================
# STREAMING OS PLATFORM AND INTERNATIONAL IMPLEMENTATION PREP BOUNDARY NOTE
# ============================================================

status: canonical-meta
system: streaming-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

# ============================================================
# 1. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

This note defines
the post-closeout boundary
for the recent platform/device support
and international support design theme
inside StreamingOS.

# ============================================================
# 2. BOUNDARY STATEMENT
# ============================================================

boundary_statement:
The recent platform/device support
and international support theme
must not return
to concept rediscovery
or broad redesign.

If later work proceeds,
it should proceed only as:
- consistency verification
- implementation preparation
- exact freeze polish
- screen / API / DDL refinement
without changing the already fixed meaning.

# ============================================================
# 3. WHAT REMAINS ALLOWED
# ============================================================

allowed_followup:
- exact API freeze refinement
- exact DDL freeze refinement
- exact screen inventory refinement
- device-specific UI planning
- localization implementation planning
- currency handling implementation planning
- implementation kickoff preparation

# ============================================================
# 4. WHAT IS NOT ALLOWED CASUALLY
# ============================================================

not_allowed_casually:
- re-scoping the theme
- removing multilingual interpretation
- removing multi-currency interpretation
- removing nation-aware currency display interpretation
- removing iPhone / Android / PC / tablet interpretation
- collapsing the fixed restart order
- re-opening completed meaning discovery

# ============================================================
# 5. SAFE RESTART ORDER
# ============================================================

safe_restart_order:
- 9005400_STREAMING_OS_PLATFORM_AND_INTERNATIONAL_REOPEN_CONTROL_NOTE.md
- 9005300_STREAMING_OS_PLATFORM_AND_INTERNATIONAL_THEME_COMPLETE_NOTE.md
- 9005200_STREAMING_OS_PLATFORM_AND_INTERNATIONAL_RESTART_FLOW_CLOSEOUT_NOTE.md
- 9005100_STREAMING_OS_PLATFORM_AND_INTERNATIONAL_RESTART_PRIORITY_ENTRY.md
- 9005000_STREAMING_OS_PLATFORM_AND_INTERNATIONAL_NEXT_CHAT_HANDOFF.md

# ============================================================
# 6. CANONICAL NOTE
# ============================================================

The recent platform/device support
and international support theme
for StreamingOS
is now closed for redesign
and open only for implementation preparation
or equivalent precision-preserving followup.

# ============================================================
# STREAMING OS PLATFORM AND INTERNATIONAL IMPLEMENTATION PREP WORKSTREAM REGISTRY
# ============================================================

status: canonical-meta
system: streaming-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

# ============================================================
# 1. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

This registry defines
the official implementation-preparation workstreams
for the recent platform/device support
and international support theme
inside StreamingOS.

# ============================================================
# 2. OFFICIAL WORKSTREAMS
# ============================================================

official_workstreams:
- workstream_01_exact_api_freeze_review
- workstream_02_exact_ddl_freeze_review
- workstream_03_device_specific_ui_planning
- workstream_04_localization_planning
- workstream_05_currency_handling_planning

# ============================================================
# 3. WORKSTREAM INTERPRETATION
# ============================================================

workstream_interpretation:
workstream_01_exact_api_freeze_review:
- review exact request payloads
- review exact response payloads
- preserve already fixed multilingual / multi-currency / device meaning

workstream_02_exact_ddl_freeze_review:
- review table / column / relation exactness
- review storage direction for multilingual / currency / device-aware meaning
- preserve already fixed theme meaning

workstream_03_device_specific_ui_planning:
- plan iPhone surfaces
- plan Android surfaces
- plan PC surfaces
- plan tablet surfaces
- preserve cross-device meaning without re-scoping

workstream_04_localization_planning:
- plan label scope
- plan wording scope
- plan locale coverage
- preserve multilingual meaning without redesign

workstream_05_currency_handling_planning:
- plan currency-aware display rules
- plan nation-aware display behavior
- plan monetary meaning vs display meaning separation
- preserve multi-currency meaning without redesign

# ============================================================
# 4. CANONICAL NOTE
# ============================================================

Implementation preparation
for this theme
must be organized through these official workstreams.

# ============================================================
# STREAMING OS PLATFORM AND INTERNATIONAL IMPLEMENTATION PREP EXECUTION ORDER
# ============================================================

status: canonical-meta
system: streaming-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

# ============================================================
# 1. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

This note defines
the official execution order
for implementation-preparation workstreams
for the recent platform/device support
and international support theme.

# ============================================================
# 2. EXECUTION ORDER
# ============================================================

execution_order:
step_01:
- workstream_01_exact_api_freeze_review

step_02:
- workstream_02_exact_ddl_freeze_review

step_03:
- workstream_03_device_specific_ui_planning

step_04:
- workstream_04_localization_planning

step_05:
- workstream_05_currency_handling_planning

# ============================================================
# 3. ORDER INTERPRETATION
# ============================================================

order_interpretation:
- API exactness should be checked first
- DDL exactness should follow API exactness
- device-specific UI planning should follow contract-side review
- localization planning should follow UI planning direction
- currency handling planning should follow core meaning preservation
  and exact structure review

# ============================================================
# 4. IMPORTANT LIMIT
# ============================================================

important_limit:
This execution order
does not allow broad redesign
or meaning rediscovery.

It only defines
the safest workstream sequence
for implementation preparation.

# ============================================================
# 5. CANONICAL NOTE
# ============================================================

A later chat should execute
implementation-preparation workstreams
through this fixed order.

# ============================================================

# ============================================================

status: canonical-meta
system: streaming-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

# ============================================================
# 1. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

This gate defines
the completion condition
for implementation-preparation work
for the recent platform/device support
and international support theme.

# ============================================================
# 2. COMPLETION CONDITION
# ============================================================

completion_condition:
Implementation-preparation work
may be considered complete only after:
- all official workstreams are reviewed
- expected deliverables are present
- fixed meaning is preserved
- redesign has not occurred
- implementation readiness is improved

# ============================================================
# 3. COMPLETION INTERPRETATION
# ============================================================

completion_interpretation:
Completion means:
- design meaning remained stable
- implementation ambiguity was reduced
- later implementation kickoff can proceed more safely

Completion does not mean:
- coding has started
- SQL has been executed
- transport has been finalized
- production rollout has started

# ============================================================
# 4. CANONICAL NOTE
# ============================================================

Implementation-preparation work
for this theme
should stop at this completion gate
before implementation begins.

# ============================================================
# STREAMING OS PLATFORM AND INTERNATIONAL IMPLEMENTATION PREP OPERATING PRINCIPLES
# ============================================================

status: canonical-meta
system: streaming-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

# ============================================================
# 1. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

This note defines
the operating principles
for implementation-preparation work
for the recent platform/device support
and international support theme.

# ============================================================
# 2. OPERATING PRINCIPLES
# ============================================================

operating_principles:
- preserve fixed meaning
- do not redesign the theme
- reduce ambiguity
- improve implementation readiness
- keep multilingual meaning explicit
- keep multi-currency meaning explicit
- keep nation-aware currency display meaning explicit
- keep cross-device meaning explicit
- write only precision-preserving followup

# ============================================================
# 3. REVIEW PRINCIPLES
# ============================================================

review_principles:
- review before changing wording
- prefer additive clarification
- avoid deleting already stabilized meaning
- do not collapse device classes
- do not collapse currency meaning into display-only wording

# ============================================================
# 4. CANONICAL NOTE
# ============================================================

Implementation-preparation work
for this theme
must follow these operating principles.

# ============================================================

status: canonical-meta
system: streaming-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

# ============================================================
# 1. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

This gate defines
when the recent platform/device support
and international support theme
may move from implementation preparation
to implementation-kickoff preparation.

# ============================================================
# 2. TRANSITION CONDITION
# ============================================================

transition_condition:
The theme may move forward only after:
- start conditions were satisfied
- official workstreams were reviewed
- expected deliverables exist
- deliverable completion requirements are satisfied
- fixed meaning remains preserved
- redesign has not occurred

# ============================================================
# 3. TRANSITION INTERPRETATION
# ============================================================

transition_interpretation:
Transition means:
- implementation preparation has done its job
- the theme is more executable
- later implementation kickoff can be planned more safely

Transition does not mean:
- code already exists
- SQL already ran
- rollout already started

# ============================================================
# 4. CANONICAL NOTE
# ============================================================

The recent platform/device support
and international support theme
for StreamingOS
may move forward
only through this transition gate.

# ============================================================
# STREAMING OS PLATFORM AND INTERNATIONAL IMPLEMENTATION KICKOFF PREP WORK TARGET REGISTRY
# ============================================================

status: canonical-meta
system: streaming-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

purpose:
Defines the official work targets
for implementation-kickoff preparation
for the recent platform/device support
and international support theme.

official_work_targets:
- implementation unit split confirmation
- coding order confirmation
- executable DDL application order confirmation
- API implementation order confirmation
- UI implementation order confirmation
- localization rollout order confirmation
- currency-handling rollout order confirmation

target_interpretation:
These targets exist
to prepare safe implementation kickoff,
not to reopen stabilized meaning.

canonical_note:
Implementation-kickoff preparation
for this theme
must be organized
through these official work targets.

# ============================================================
# STREAMING OS PLATFORM AND INTERNATIONAL IMPLEMENTATION KICKOFF PREP KICKOFF START GATE
# ============================================================

status: canonical-meta
system: streaming-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

purpose:
Defines the kickoff start gate
for implementation-kickoff preparation
for the recent platform/device support
and international support theme.

kickoff_start_gate:
Implementation-kickoff preparation
may start only after:
- implementation-prep transition gate satisfied
- kickoff-prep start conditions satisfied
- official restart order understood
- official work targets understood

important_limit:
This gate does not indicate
that coding has started.

canonical_note:
Implementation-kickoff preparation
for this theme
must begin only through this kickoff start gate.

# ============================================================
# STREAMING OS PLATFORM AND INTERNATIONAL IMPLEMENTATION GO NO-GO GATE
# ============================================================

status: canonical-meta
system: streaming-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

# ============================================================
# 1. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

This gate defines
the formal go / no-go condition
before actual implementation start
for the recent platform/device support
and international support theme
inside StreamingOS.

# ============================================================
# 2. GO CONDITION
# ============================================================

go_condition:
Actual implementation may be considered
only after all of the following are true:
- implementation-prep transition gate satisfied
- implementation-kickoff prep start gate satisfied
- kickoff-prep work target registry reviewed
- kickoff-prep first work targets reviewed
- fixed multilingual meaning preserved
- fixed multi-currency meaning preserved
- fixed nation-aware currency display meaning preserved
- fixed cross-device meaning preserved
- no broad redesign occurred

# ============================================================
# 3. NO-GO CONDITION
# ============================================================

no_go_condition:
Implementation must not start if:
- any required gate is missing
- any required deliverable is missing
- meaning drift occurred
- device scope drift occurred
- currency meaning drift occurred
- language scope drift occurred
- execution order is still ambiguous

# ============================================================
# 4. IMPORTANT LIMIT
# ============================================================

important_limit:
This document does not itself start implementation.
It only defines the formal decision boundary
for whether implementation may begin.

# ============================================================
# 5. CANONICAL NOTE
# ============================================================

The recent platform/device support
and international support theme
for StreamingOS
must pass this go / no-go gate
before actual implementation start.

# ============================================================
# STREAMING OS PLATFORM AND INTERNATIONAL FINAL NEXT CHAT HANDOFF
# ============================================================

status: canonical-handoff
system: streaming-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

# ============================================================
# 1. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

This document is the final next-chat handoff
for the recent platform/device support
and international support theme
inside StreamingOS.

It exists so that a later chat
can restart safely
without rediscovering meaning,
without reopening closed scope,
and without losing the current stage boundary.

# ============================================================
# 2. CURRENT FIXED STATE
# ============================================================

current_fixed_state:
- multilingual operation fixed
- multi-currency handling fixed
- nation-aware currency display fixed
- iPhone support fixed
- Android support fixed
- PC support fixed
- tablet support fixed
- redesign blocked
- implementation preparation structured
- implementation-kickoff preparation structured
- actual implementation not yet started

# ============================================================
# 3. OPEN FIRST IN NEXT CHAT
# ============================================================

and international support theme
